   <h2>Metadata</h2>
   <dl class="grid">
      <dt>Name:</dt>
      <dd>mkn-kurrent-gt</dd>
      <dt>Description:</dt>
      <dd>Kurrent GT from the Moravian Knowledge Network handwritten periodicals</dd>
      <dt>Language:</dt>
      <dd>deu</dd>
      <dt>Format:</dt>
      <dd>Page-XML</dd>
      <dt>Time:</dt>
      <dd>1765-1806</dd>
      <dt>GT Type:</dt>
      <dd>data_structure_and_text</dd>
   </dl>
   <details>
      <summary>More Information</summary>
      <dl class="more-grid">
